<span class="poetry indentAll">Such is the circle<sup class="footnote-marker">b</sup><i class="footnote"><b>circle </b>Lit. “generation.”</i> of those who turn to You,<sup class="footnote-marker">c</sup><i class="footnote"><b>You </b>Heb. 3rd person.</i> </span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">Jacob, who seek Your presence. <i>   Selah.</i> </span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">O gates, lift up your heads!</span><br><span class="poetry indentAll">Up high, you everlasting doors,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">so the King<sup class="footnote-marker">d</sup><i class="footnote"><b>King </b>I.e., the One who leads the celestial army.</i> of glory may come in!</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">Who is the King of glory?—</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">
G<small>OD</small>, mighty and valiant,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble"> 
G<small>OD</small>, valiant in battle.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">O gates, lift up your heads!</span><br><span class="poetry indentAll">Lift them up, you everlasting doors,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">so the King of glory may come in!</span>

G<small>OD</small>
 of Hosts</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">is truly the King of glory! <i>   Selah.</i> </span>

Chapter 25

Of David.<br><span class="poetry indentAll"> <b>א</b> O E<small>TERNAL</small> One, I set my hope on You;</span>
<span class="poetry indentAllDouble"><b>ב</b> my God, in You I trust;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">may I not be disappointed,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">may my enemies not exult over me.</span><br><span class="poetry indentAll"> </span>

Chapter 26

Of David.<br><span class="poetry indentAll">Vindicate me, O E<small>TERNAL</small> One,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">for I have walked without blame;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">I have trusted in G<small>OD</small>;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">I have not faltered.</span>

<span class="poetry indentAll">I do not consort with scoundrels,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">or mix with hypocrites;</span>
<span class="poetry indentAllDouble">I detest the company of evildoers,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">and do not consort with the wicked;</span>

<span class="poetry indentAll">My feet are on level ground.</span><br><span class="poetry indentAll">In assemblies I will bless G<small>OD</small>.</span>

Chapter 27

Of David.<br><span class="poetry indentAll"> 
G<small>OD</small>
 is my light and my help;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">whom should I fear?</span><br><span class="poetry indentAll">

Chapter 30

A psalm of David. A song for the dedication of the House.<sup class="footnote-marker">a</sup><i class="footnote"><b>the House </b>I.e., the temple.</i> 
<span class="poetry indentAll">I extol You, O E<small>TERNAL</small> One,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">for You have lifted me up,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">and not let my enemies rejoice over me.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">O my E<small>TERNAL</small> God,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">I cried out to You,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">and You healed me.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">O E<small>TERNAL</small> One, You brought me up from Sheol,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">preserved me from going down into the Pit.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">O you faithful of G<small>OD</small>, sing out,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">and praise the holy name.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">For [God] is angry but a moment,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">and when pleased, there is life.</span><br><span class="poetry indentAll">One may lie down weeping at nightfall;<sup class="footnote-marker">b</sup><i class="footnote"><b>One may lie down weeping at nightfall </b>Or “Weeping may linger for the night.”</i> </span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">but at dawn there are shouts of joy.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">When I was untroubled,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">I thought, “I shall never be shaken,”</span>
<span class="poetry indentAllDouble">for You, O E<small>TERNAL</small> One, when You were pleased,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">made [me]<sup class="footnote-marker">c</sup><i class="footnote"><b>[me] </b>Following Saadia, R. Isaiah of Trani; cf. Ibn Ezra.</i> firm as a mighty mountain.</span><br><span class="poetry indentAll">When You hid Your face,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">I was terrified.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">I called to You, O E<small>TERNAL</small> One;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">to my Sovereign I made appeal,</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">“What is to be gained from my death,<sup class="footnote-marker">d</sup><i class="footnote"><b>death </b>Lit. “blood.”</i> </span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">from my descent into the Pit?</span><br><span class="poetry indentAll">Can dust praise You?</span><br><span class="poetry indentAll">Can it declare Your faithfulness?</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">Hear, O E<small>TERNAL</small> One, and have mercy on me;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">O E<small>TERNAL</small> One, be my help!”</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">You turned my lament into dancing,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">you undid my sackcloth and girded me with joy,</span>
<span class="poetry indentAllDouble">that [my] whole being might sing hymns to You endlessly;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">O my E<small>TERNAL</small> God, I will praise You forever.</span>

Chapter 31

For the leader. A psalm of David.
<span class="poetry indentAll">I seek refuge in You, O E<small>TERNAL</small> One;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">may I never be disappointed;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">as You are righteous, rescue me.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">Incline Your ear to me;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">be quick to save me;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">be a rock, a stronghold for me,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">a citadel, for my deliverance.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">For You are my rock and my fortress;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">You lead me and guide me as befits Your name.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">You free me from the net laid for me,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">for You are my stronghold.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">Into Your hand I entrust my spirit;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">You redeem me, O E<small>TERNAL</small> One, faithful God.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">I detest those who rely on empty folly,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">but I trust in G<small>OD</small>.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">Let me exult and rejoice in Your faithfulness</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">when You notice my affliction,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">are mindful of my deep distress,</span>
<span class="poetry indentAllDouble">and do not hand me over to my enemy,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">but grant me relief.<sup class="footnote-marker">a</sup><i class="footnote"><b>grant me relief </b>Lit. “make my feet stand in a broad place.”</i> </span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">Have mercy on me, O E<small>TERNAL</small> One,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">for I am in distress;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">my eyes are wasted by vexation,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">my substance and body too.<sup class="footnote-marker">b</sup><i class="footnote"><b>my substance and body too </b>Meaning of Heb. uncertain.</i> </span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">My life is spent in sorrow,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">my years in groaning;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">my strength fails because of my iniquity,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">my limbs waste away.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">Because of all my foes</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">I am the particular butt of my neighbors,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">a horror to my friends;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">those who see me on the street avoid me.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">I am put out of mind like the dead;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">I am like an object given up for lost.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">I hear the whisperings of many,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">intrigue<sup class="footnote-marker">c</sup><i class="footnote"><b>intrigue </b>In contrast to others “terror.”</i> on every side,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">as they scheme together against me,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">plotting to take my life.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">But I trust in You, O E<small>TERNAL</small> One;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">I say, “You are my God!”</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">My fate is in Your hand;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">save me from the hand of my enemies and pursuers.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">Show favor to Your servant;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">as You are faithful, deliver me.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">O E<small>TERNAL</small> One, let me not be disappointed when I call You;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">let the wicked be disappointed;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">let them be silenced in Sheol;</span>
<span class="poetry indentAllDouble">let lying lips be stilled</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">that speak haughtily against the righteous</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">with arrogance and contempt.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">How abundant is the good</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">that You have in store for those who fear You,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">that You do in full view</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">for those who take refuge in You.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">You grant them the protection of Your presence</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">against the opposition’s schemes;<sup class="footnote-marker">d</sup><i class="footnote"><b>against the opposition’s schemes </b>Or “against human schemes.” Meaning of Heb. uncertain.</i> </span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">You shelter them in Your pavilion</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">from contentious tongues.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">Blessed is G<small>OD</small>,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">who has been wondrously faithful to me,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">a veritable bastion.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">Alarmed, I had thought,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">“I am thrust out of Your sight”;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">yet You listened to my plea for mercy</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">when I cried out to You.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">So love G<small>OD</small>, all you faithful;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble"> 
G<small>OD</small>
 guards the loyal,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">and more than requites</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">the one who acts arrogantly.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">Be strong and of good courage,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">all you who wait for G<small>OD</small>.</span>

Chapter 32

Of David. A <i>maskil</i>.<sup class="footnote-marker">a</sup><i class="footnote"><b><i>maskil</i> </b>Meaning of Heb. uncertain.</i> <br><span class="poetry indentAll">Happy is the one whose transgression is forgiven,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">whose sin is covered over.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">Happy the person whom G<small>OD</small> does not hold guilty,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">and in whose spirit there is no deceit.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">As long as I said nothing,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">my limbs wasted away</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">from my anguished roaring all day long.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">For night and day</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">Your hand lay heavy on me;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">my vigor waned</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">as in the summer drought. <i>   Selah.</i> </span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">Then I acknowledged my sin to You;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">I did not cover up my guilt;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">I resolved, “I will confess my transgressions to G<small>OD</small>,”</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">and You forgave the guilt of my sin. <i>   Selah.</i> </span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">Therefore let all the faithful pray to You</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">upon discovering [their sin],<sup class="footnote-marker">b</sup><i class="footnote"><b>upon discovering [their sin] </b>Meaning of Heb. uncertain; in contrast to others “in a time when You may be found.”</i> </span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">that the rushing mighty waters</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">not overtake them.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">You are my shelter;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">You preserve me from distress;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">You surround me with the joyous shouts of deliverance. <i>   Selah.</i> </span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">Let me enlighten you</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">and show you which way to go;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">let me offer counsel; my eye is on you.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">Be not like a senseless horse or mule</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">whose movement must be curbed by bit and bridle;<sup class="footnote-marker">c</sup><i class="footnote"><b>whose movement must be curbed by bit and bridle </b>Meaning of Heb. uncertain.</i> </span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">far be it from you!<sup class="footnote-marker">d</sup><i class="footnote"><b>far be it from you </b>Meaning of Heb. uncertain; for this rendering cf. Ibn Ezra.</i> </span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">Many are the torments of the wicked,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">but those who trust in G<small>OD</small> </span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">shall be surrounded with favor.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">Rejoice in G<small>OD</small> and exult, O you righteous;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">shout for joy, all the upright!</span>

Chapter 33

<span class="poetry indentAll">Sing forth, O you righteous, to G<small>OD</small>;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">it is fitting that the upright offer praise.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">Praise G<small>OD</small> with the lyre;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">with the ten-stringed harp sing out;</span>
<span class="poetry indentAllDouble">sing [God] a new song;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">play sweetly with shouts of joy.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">For the word of G<small>OD</small> is right,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">and God’s every deed is faithful.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">[God] loves what is right and just;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">the earth is full of G<small>OD</small>’s faithful care.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">By the word of G<small>OD</small> the heavens were made,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">by the breath of God’s mouth, all their host.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">[God] heaps up the ocean waters like a mound,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">stores the deep in vaults.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">Let all the earth fear G<small>OD</small>;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">let all the inhabitants of the world feel dread.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">For [God] spoke, and it was;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">issued the command, and it endured.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">
G<small>OD</small>
 frustrates the plans of nations,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">brings to naught the designs of peoples.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">What G<small>OD</small> plans endures forever,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">what [God] designs, for ages on end.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">Happy the nation whose God is the E<small>TERNAL</small>,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">the people who are chosen as a permanent possession.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">
G<small>OD</small>
 looks down from heaven</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">and sees all humankind.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">From God’s dwelling-place the divine gaze touches</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">on all the inhabitants of the earth—</span>
<span class="poetry indentAllDouble">the One who fashions the hearts of them all,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">who discerns all their doings.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">Kings are not delivered by a large force;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">warriors are not saved by great strength;</span>
<span class="poetry indentAllDouble">horses are a false hope for deliverance;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">for all their great power they provide no escape.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">Truly G<small>OD</small>’s eye is on those who show reverence,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">who wait for God’s faithful care</span>
<span class="poetry indentAllDouble">to save them from death,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">to sustain them in famine.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">We set our hope on G<small>OD</small>,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">who is our help and shield;</span>
<span class="poetry indentAllDouble">in whom our hearts rejoice,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">in whose holy name we trust.</span>
<span class="poetry indentAll">May we enjoy, O E<small>TERNAL</small> One, Your faithful care,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">as we have put our hope in You.</span>

Chapter 34

Of David, when he feigned madness in the presence of Abimelech, who turned him out, and he left.<sup class="footnote-marker">a</sup><i class="footnote"><b>when he feigned madness … and he left </b>Cf. <a class="refLink" data-ref="I Samuel 21:14" href="I_Samuel.21.14">1 Sam. 21.14ff</a>.</i> <br><span class="poetry indentAll"> </span>
<span class="poetry indentAll"><b>א</b> I bless G<small>OD</small> at all times;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">praise is ever in my mouth.</span><br><span class="poetry indentAll"> </span>
<span class="poetry indentAll"><b>ב</b> I glory in G<small>OD</small>;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">let the lowly hear it and rejoice.</span><br><span class="poetry indentAll"> </span>
<span class="poetry indentAll"><b>ג</b> Exalt G<small>OD</small> with me;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">let us extol the divine name together.</span><br><span class="poetry indentAll"> </span>
<span class="poetry indentAll"><b>ד</b> I turned to G<small>OD</small>, and I was answered;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">I was saved from all my terrors.</span><br><span class="poetry indentAll"> </span>
<span class="poetry indentAll"><b>ה</b> People look to [God] and are radiant;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAll"> </span>
<span class="poetry indentAll"><b>ו</b> <b>ז</b> Here was a lowly man who called—</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">
G<small>OD</small>

<span class="poetry indentAll"><b>ח</b> The angel of G<small>OD</small> camps around those who show awe,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">and rescues them.</span><br><span class="poetry indentAll"> </span>
<span class="poetry indentAll"><b>ט</b> Taste and see how good G<small>OD</small> is;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">happy the one<sup class="footnote-marker">b</sup><i class="footnote"><b>one </b>Or “virile man.”</i> who takes refuge in the divine!</span><br><span class="poetry indentAll"> </span>
<span class="poetry indentAll"><b>י</b> Fear the E<small>TERNAL</small>, you consecrated ones,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">for those who fear [God] lack nothing.</span><br><span class="poetry indentAll"> </span>
<span class="poetry indentAll"><b>כ</b> Lions have been reduced to starvation,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">but those who turn to G<small>OD</small> shall not lack any good.</span><br><span class="poetry indentAll"> </span>
<span class="poetry indentAll"><b>ל</b> Come, my children, listen to me;</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">I will teach you what it is to fear G<small>OD</small>.</span><br><span class="poetry indentAll"> </span>

<span class="poetry indentAll"><b>נ</b> Guard your tongue from evil,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">your lips from deceitful speech.</span><br><span class="poetry indentAll"> </span>
<span class="poetry indentAll"><b>ס</b> Shun evil and do good,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">seek amity<sup class="footnote-marker">c</sup><i class="footnote"><b>amity </b>Or “integrity.”</i> and pursue it.</span><br><span class="poetry indentAll"> </span>
<span class="poetry indentAll"><b>ע</b> G<small>OD</small>’s eyes are on the righteous,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">the ears, attentive to their cry.</span><br><span class="poetry indentAll"> </span>
<span class="poetry indentAll"><b>פ</b> G<small>OD</small>’s face is set against evildoers,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">to erase their names from the earth.</span><br><span class="poetry indentAll"> </span>
<span class="poetry indentAll"><b>צ</b> They<sup class="footnote-marker">d</sup><i class="footnote"><b>They </b>Namely, the righteous of v. <a class="refLink" data-ref="Psalms 34:16" href="Psalms.34.16">16</a>.</i> cry out, and G<small>OD</small> hears,</span><br><span class="poetry indentAllDouble">and saves them from all their troubles.</span><br><span class="poetry indentAll"> </span>
